msg:A very satisfying experience. I originally planned to split the villa, but the hotel upgraded it to the main building, which is closer to the hot springs.

Room: The scenery is good. I took pictures of the sunrise from the balcony in the morning. If there is sunset, the orientation of the room will be better. The bed was of moderate softness and firmness. It was quiet at night and I slept very comfortably. The quilt and pillows are also very comfortable. I plan to come back with my family in the future.

Hot springs: There are many different pools. There are not many people on weekdays. I think the current temperature is just right for a hot spring bath. The water park is closed and there is no place for children to play. Adults are happy to soak in different pools and use saunas. The locker room is very hygienic and the staff are constantly wiping water off the floor. You can enter unlimited times when you stay in the hotel. We checked in in the afternoon, went for a dip before dinner, once after dinner, and again the next morning. We were happy.

Buffet breakfast: There is freshly ground coffee, cereals, bread, fried dough sticks, chicken popcorn, pasta, cheong fun, sausages, salads, salads, fruits, desserts, yogurt, etc. There are both Chinese and Western food, and some have local characteristics, such as sausages and noodles. , tofu pudding. When I left, I also gave away two boxes of tofu pudding, which I could eat and take with me.

Service: Great. Problems can be solved proactively. Every staff member I met has a very good attitude. They gave me welcome fruits and snacks when I came, and a bag of sweet potatoes when I left.

Surroundings: There are many farm dishes and milk tea within 10 minutes of walking out of the hotel. They all taste good and are very suitable for vacation.

The regret is that we came by bus. It is inconvenient to go to Dafengmen Scenic Area without a car. The complimentary tickets can only be wasted. Next time, the family will come by car (‚âß‚ñΩ‚â¶)
